47-50. PLANETARY STAGES (aur or waeat) AND
EFFECTS THEREOF: It is boyhood (ata) if a planet isin
its own house or friendly house. In Mulatrikona Rasi, it is
in youth (gHr<) and in adolescence (gaf) in exaltation.
It is said to be in old stage (ggraear) if it occupies an inimical
house. A planet in debilitation is im extremis (we). The
corresponding effects are felt in the respective planetary dasas
ie. periods. The results for such stages are respectively
happiness, virtue, kingdom, sickness with debts, and death or
expenses.

Notes : The zat or qaear explained above are by virtue

of a planet’s occupying different Rasis. Jataka Tatwa (A-68
and 69) states a different rule. In odd signs, according to the
longitude obtained by the planet, itis in infancy, boyhood,
## Page 84

80. Saravali

adolescence, advanced age and in extremis, Each Rasi is to
be made in 5 parts of 6° cach. This order is reverse in the
case of even signs, ie. “infancy” is at the end, preceded by
boyhood and so on and so forth. A planet in adolescent stage
is capable of giving full results (i.e. 12° 1’ to 18° of odd or even
Rasi).

51-52. EFFECTS OF PLANETS IN ODD AND EVEN

RASIS : A planet in odd Rasi with strength makes the native
courageous and a warrior. If itis weak in odd Rasi, the
native is cruel and dullwitted. A planet in even Rasi gives soft
nature, fear for quarrels, love for water, flowers and clothes,
good fortune, health and protection of own men.

1, KARAKA PLANETS (PLANETARY CO-WORKERS) :
Planets posited in own house, Mulatrikona or exaltation and
## Page 85

Chapter 6 81

simultaneously in (mutual) angles become mutual Karakas
or significators. Such kind of yoga Karakas (co-workers)
arecounted only in regard to Lagna’s angles. This view is held
by Acharya Hari.

cleat area: Heiteart agetfafenty
Re get cage: ceed aTeT TAN
2. For example, Saturn in Libra while Cancer ascends

containing Jupiter and the Moon, and Mars with the Sun in
Aries become mutual Karakas.

Notes : In the said example given by our author, Cancer
ascendant has Moon in own house and Jupiter in exaltation;
Saturn is exalted in Libra, the 4th from Lagaa while Mars is
in own house in 10th andthe Sun .is exalted in the 10th in
Aries. Thus, these 5 planets are mutually in angles and either
in exaltation or in own house. Hence they promote the mutual
significations and act favouring the native. Now, see the chart
as per the sloka :

[Lagna
Jup
Moon|

Some authors (not Kalyana Varma) say that planets
mutully angular though not being so from ascendant, become
mutual signifactors. But this view is not acceptable to even
Chanakya. Kalyana Varma clearly requires the planets to be
in angles only from the ascendant and not even from the Moon,
not to speak of non-angular state from the ascendant. Horasara,
Ch. 16, sloka 11, however takes into consideration such mutua
## Page 86

82 Saravalt

angularity irrespective of Lagna at birth, Now, we have to
understand what is the effect of such Karakatwa, By being in
such Vargas and also in angles from Lagna, two planets act on
behalf of each other. In the example case, though Saturn is the
lord of the 8th and evil for Cancer, he will reflect the qualities
of other good planets, say Moon-Sun and promotes the pros-
perity. Neither the mutual aspect between the Sun and Saturn
shall be adverse in this case.

5-6, EFFECTS OF (YOGA) KARAKAS (CO-WORKERS):
Even though a person may be born in base strata, he will
become chief if he has Karaka Grahas. One born in royal
family without doubt becomes a king, in sucha case. While

analysing the Yogas, such Karakatwas are alone important and
effects should be declared only on that basis.

Chapter 7 Planetary Indications

1, LORD OF WEEK DAY ETC: The Sun, the Moon,
Mars, Mercury, Jupiter, Venus and Siturn rule the week days
etc, Whichever planet becomes the lord of the first week day in
the month of Aswinain the year of Aswina, will become the
lord of month and year.

Notes : Whichever planet rules the opening week day of
the year shall be the year lord. That is, ifa year starts on
Monday (ruled by the Moon), the year lord is Moon. Similarly
whoever rules the first weck day of a month, is designated
as lord of the month.

weafaarsagat: FAM Teste TAIT: |

weafat: sareqr wafer: sara ey ua

2.3. The fourth planet counted from the lord of the
first year rules the second year. Similar counting of fourth
lords for the subsequent years should be made to know the
lords thereof, There are 24 horas (i.c. planetary hours) in
each day (from one Sun-rise to the next Sun-rise). The first
Hora is ruled by the lord of the week day while the subsequent
ones are ruled by the lords of the sixth week days thereof,
Thirty (Savana) days make one (Savana) month. To know the
Jord of the week day in particular month, the months past
should be multiplied by 30, increased by one and divided by 7.
The remainder represents the lord of the week day counted from
the earlier week day lord.
## Page 88

84 Saravali

upleangaridaaraatier-aerdtary tl
arat fear grasfrasrdearary us

4, A Savana month has 30 days and each month, viz.
Chaitra, Vaisakha etc, commences with the first day of Bright
half and ends with the 30th thithi (i.e. New Moon's day or
Amavasya).

5-6. BHAVA EFFECTS : The good effects relating to a
bhava can be better reaped if an enterprise relating to that
bhava is started inan ascendant ruled by the lord of that
bhava, or when the lord thereof is in an upachaya house, or on
the week day, Hora, year or month ruled by that bhava lord,
The good effects will be 25% by year lord, 50% by month
lord, 75% by lord of week day and 100% by hora lord.

Notes : Suppose one wants to buy a conveyance. This
aspect is ruled by the 4th lord. Let us assume it is Mercury,
Hence a hora ruled by Mercury will be 100% beneficial for that
purpose. Alternatively an ascendant ruled by Mercury, or

when he is in 3, 6, 10 or 11 of another ascendant may also be
useful.

7-13. PLANET’S RULERSHIPS : The Sun rules snakes,
wool, hills, gold, weapons, poison, fire, medicines, kings,
Aryas (or foreigners in general), river banks, forest, wood and
Mantras, The Moon indicates poets, flowers, eatables, beads,
silver, conch, salt, water, arrow, robes, ornaments, females,
ghee, sesamum, oil and sleep. Mars rules blood, copper, army,
red cloth, mercury, minerals, earth, king, destruction, swoon-
ing, bile and thieves. Mercury rules Vedas, writing, sculpture,
medicines, expertise, ministership, speech, jokes, birds, couples,
fame, Vanaspathi (ie. a large forest tree which bears fruit
apparently without any blossoms) and gold. Jupiter rules
auspiciousness, virtue, physical stoutness, prowess, preceptor-
ship, deputation, city, state (province), gold, bed, conveyance,
Position, grains, residence and sons. Venus rules diamonds,
ornaments, matriage, scents, friends, wreaths, females, cow
dung, diagnosis (frata apart from meaning diagnosis also
indicates end, purity, rope to tying up a calf etc.), education,
sexual enjoyment (frgad), and gold. Saturn is Karaka for
lead, zine, black metals, inferior grains, dead relatives, fools,
servants, mean women, salable goods (quq%), servants, poor
people and self restraint. (Ztet apart from meaning self rest-
raint also means investing with sacred thread which is in vogue
to give “‘second birth” to Brahmins).

14-15. PLANETARY PLACES : The Sun rules Kalinga
(a Coromandel district), the Moon Yavana (Greek, Mohamme-
dan or European countries), Venus plain river banks, Jupiter
Sindhu (Indus), Mercury Magadha (southern part of Bihar),
Saturn Saurashtra (Gujrat), Mars Ujjain and the nodes i.e.
Rahu and Ketu Dravida country (ic. five tribes: Dravida,
Karnataka, Goorjara, Maharashtra and Tailenga).

Notes : The reader is profitably referred to Brihat
Samhita of Varaha Mihira (Ch, 16) for detailed planetary ruler-
ships of countries, rivers, objects etc. Such information may
be quite useful in predictive astrology and mundane astrology
as well.

Chapter 8 Copulation (And Conception)
crearfanafian: ea faaet fear aqeafar
aIaTTAAAT aay BILUTYS AACATGATT EU

1-3, A FEMALE’S MENSTRUATION; Without the know-
ledge of conception time, one cannot understand the effects of
the various divisions like Rasi. That is why I explain below
about conception which is the cause of births of all animals.

Asa result of Moon’s transit in Anupachaya Rasis and in

aspect to Mars, a female obtains her menses. The Moon is

water and Mars is fire; water produces blood and fire produces

bile, When bile is enraged by blood, the women gets her
menstiuation.
## Page 91

Chapter 8 87

Notes : Anupachaya Rasis are the houses other than the
upachayas. The former are: Ist, 2nd, 4th, Sth, 7th, 8th, 9th
and 12th while the latter are 3rd, 6th, 10th and 11th. The
Moon in Anupachya house and in aspect to Mars while in
transit can cause attainment of puberty or the regular monthly
course toa female. The Moon in upachaya should be aspected
by Jupiter so that the intercourse at that time leads to fruition
of conception. Please see Horasara, p. 41 for more relevant
information.

va aquafa wit aaea fafeata wfad aq!
grades fan sfama aid vet yn

qat wife oat falas: yadeuy
we ge ee qeradt ag fae aataq)
uegeam waar vata qa
aaa wel caress arsed: garfefa: Ga: 1
ea: eaqg carat wegft Feared gafa: ue

4-1. The menstruation so caused makes the female capable
of conception. If the Moon is in upachaya (i. e. 3, 6, 10 and
11), it makes the menses defunct for conception. However, if
the Moon in upachaya is aspected by Jupiter or her friends, or
especially Venus, the woman affectionately cohabits with the
male. If the Moon is aspected by Mars, the female unites with
a person other than husband. The Sun if aspecting the Moon
indicates a king while Saturn aspecting “denotes a servant.
Similar inferences should be made if the Moon is aspected by
malefics only, without aspect of benefics. If the Moon is
aspected by malefics like Mars, then the female gives up her
home and becomes a prostitute.

Notes : If the Moon is in upachaya but without the aspect
of Jupiter, the monthly course at that time does not promote the
chance of conception. The other conditions mentioned in these
slokas relate to planetary positions at the time of a girl's
attaining puberty. (These should not be over-enthusiastically
applied to one’s regular menses, for some planet or other possibly
## Page 92

88 Saravalt

may lend aspect to the Moon, many times when the female gets
her monthly course.) The first menses has great bearing on the
future of her married life and in olden days (even now in many
parts of the country), Ritu Jataka, is cast for the time of
puberty. If in the Ritu Jataka. the Moon being aspected by
Venus or Mars or Saturn and so on, varius results as attri-
buted will come to pass. Similarly, there are specific effects for
a girl's attaining puberty on a particular week day, Nakshatra,
Karana, Yoga, Tithi, in a particular ascendant and in particular
lunar month, For example, puberty occurring while Bharani
star rules causes abortions, immorality, barrenness etc. It is
inauspicious at the time of Sun-rise, twilights, eclipses, Full
Moon days Sun-set, New Moon day,solar ingressions etc. In
Aries Ascendant, she becomes adulterous. Similarly in
Scorpio Ascendant. Pisces rising bestows a number of children.
Such useful information can be elicited from the various
classics like Muhurta Darpana, Jyotisha Ratna-mala etc.

8-10. The 7th house from Lagna at the time of copulation
indicates the disposition of the couple. If there is a malefic’s
aspect to the Lagna at the time of copulation, the couple unites
angrily and with quarrel. Should it be benefic’s aspect, then the
sexual enjoyment will be (pleasing) as enumerated by Vatsya-
yana Maharshi. If there be both malefic and benefic aspects on
the 7ih, the sexual act is mixed in nature. According to one’s
past deeds, to ripe its fruits, the semen enters the womb and
conception ensues.

Notes : The author gives tips to choose a proper time for
sexual intercourse, so that it confers happiness. Benific’s aspect
to the 7th house from the ascendant prevailing at that time
## Page 93

Chapter 8 89
leads to a happy sexual act while a malefic’s aspect does not,
Benefic’s aspect to such Lagna causes conception while mixed
aspect makes it both unhappy and happy. According to one’s
past deeds, at the destined moment, the semen enters the womb
of a female and conception ensues, so that the soul which already
Formed part of the semen, reaps the results in its current birth.

11-12. OCCURRENCE OF PREGNANCY : If the transit
Sun and Venus be in upachaya Rasis (3, 6, 10 and 11th), with
strength, with reference to the male partner’s nativity and
occupy even Navamsas, there is scope of pregnancy to be caused
by the particular intercourse. Similar effects follow if strong
‘Moon and strong Mars be in upachaya Rasis in transit with
reference to the female’s horocope and be in even Navamsas.
Alternatively, Venus, Sun, Mars and Moon should be in upa-
chaya houses in own Amsas or Jupiter be in Lagna, Sth or 9th
with strength to cause pregnancy.

Notes: In the transit Rasi chart, the Sun and Venus
should be in 3rd, 6th, 10th or 11th from his natal ascendant
and should occupy even Navamsas, like Taurus, Cancer, Virgo
etc. Such an intercourse will lead to conception. Similarly,
Mars and the Moon should be in Upachaya Rasi and in even
Navamsa for a female. The third and fourth conditions are
simple.

It is worthwhile noting what Varaha Mihira denotes in
his Brihat Samhita about coition, in the context of obtaining
children : The woman should bathe on the fourth day of menses
with the herbs mentioned (in Ch. XLVI ibid) and the hymns
cited (in slokas 55-70 ibid) should be recited. After this, she
should have a union with her loving husband to get a male
child in even nights, or to get a female child in odd nights. If it
is more distant even nights (before the 16th night), it leads to
birth of longliving, handsome and happy son. So to say, if the
## Page 94

90 Saravali

Adhana is, for example, in the 6th, 8th, 10th night etc. it leads
to acquisition ofa male issue while an intercourse on the Sth,
7th, 9th night etc. promotes the birth of female child. The man
should have sexual union when angles and trines are benefic-
occupied, when the ascendant/Moon are with benefics and
when malefics are in 3, 6 and 11th houses and when there are
planetary indications to ensure obtainment of progeny.
Curious reader may consult Brihat Samhita for fuller in-
structions on this count.

Then, Balabhadra inhis Hora Ratna observes on our
present sloka of Saravali thus: The Sun in Upachaya houses
(3, 6,10 or 11) promotes the masculine vigour of a preson
while Venus so positioned strengthens his virility. Fora male,
the Sun's strength is essential. Mars rules blood which produces
menses in a woman. The Moon’s potence is essential for a
woman and hence she should have these in Upachayas.

Suka Jataka adds that the Sun and Venus should be in
their Navamas while in Upachaya for a male. And Mars and
Moon should be in their Navamsas for a female. In both cases,
Upachaya Rasi positions are necessary.

13. DISPOSITION OF FOETUS : The child in the womb

will be according to the mental disposition of the couple and
their desires and according to Tridoshas (bile, phlegm and wind)
prevailing.

Notes : According to Sastras, the woman should sexually
join her husband lovingly, with a desire to beget an offspring.
The couple should be well-disposed towards each other,

14-15. SEX OF THE CHILD : Should Lagna, Moon,
Jupiter and the Sun be strong and be in male Rasis and male
## Page 95

Chapter 8 91

Navamsas, birth of a male child be predicted. If they are in
even Rasis and even Amsas, predict female child. If strong
Jupiter and Sun be in male Rasis, male child will be born.
Female child should be expected if Venus, Moon and Mars are
in even Rasis.

Notes : From this sloka onwards, till the end of this
chapter, all Lagna references should be related to Adhana
(srara) unless otherwise mentioned.

16. TWIN BIRTH: If the Sun and Jupiter be in Gemini or
Sagittarius in aspect to Mercury, birth of two male children be
predicted. Two female children will be born if Venus, Mars
and the Moon be in Pisces or Virgo in aspect Mercury.

than Lagna, a male child will be born. Such yogasand strengths
at the time of Adhana should be properly assessed to predict
birth of male or female child.

18-20. BIRTH OF HERMAPHRODITE : Birth of a
hermaphrodite should be declared if the Sun and the Moon be
in odd Rasis and be in mutual aspect, or if Mercury and Saturn
be in mutual aspect from odd Rasis, or if Mars aspects the Sun
who is in an even Rasi, or if the Moon is in Lagna in odd Rasi.

‘These are the views of sages. If Mars aspects Mercury in odd
Rasi and simultaneously the Moon in even Rasi, same effect
## Page 96

92 Saravali

follows. Alternatively if Lagna, Moon and Mercury be in odd
Rasi and odd Navamsa and aspected by Venus and Saturn,
eunuch birth is indicated.

21-22. ONE MALE CHILD AND ONE FEMALE CHILD

TO BE BORN : Should Lagna and Moon be in even Rasis and
be aspected by a strong planet, then there are twins in the womb
(one male child and one female child). Similar results follow if
the Moon and Venus are in even Rasis while Jupiter, Mars,
Mercury and Lagna be in odd Rasis or common signs and be
strong.

23-26. BIRTH OF TRIPLETS : The following yogas
pervailing at the time of Adhana lead to births of triplets :
(@) Mercury remaining in Gemini Navamsa aspecting a planet
who also falls in common Navamsa (b) Mercury remaining in
Gemini Navamsa aspecting a common sign which ascends (c)
Mercury in Virgo Navamsa aspecting a planet falling in
common Navamsa (d) Mercury in Virgo Navamsa aspecting
acommon sign which ascends (ce) Mercury in Gemini Amsa
aspecting a planet in Gemini Amsa or Sagittarius Amsa (f)
Mercury in Gemini Navamsa aspecting the Lagna which falls in
Gemini Navamsa or Sagittarius Navamsa, (g) Mercury in 7th
aspecting a planet in Kanya or Mina Navamsa or aspecting
## Page 97

Chapter 8 93

such Lagna Navamsa. Combinations (a) and (b) lead to birth
of triplets-one female and two males. Combinations (c) and
(d) cause birth of triplets consisting of two females and one
male. Combinations at (e) and (f) cause three male children
while the ones at (g) indicate three female children.

27. MOTHER, FATHER, ETC. : If births take place
in day time Venus indicates mother while the Sun indicates
father. In the case of nights the Moon and Saturn respectively
play these roles. Similarly the Moon denotes mother’s sister
and Saturn paternal uncle for day time births while Venus
and the Sun take over these portfolios respectively in the case
of night births.

28. EFFECTS OF SUCH PLANETS : If the planets deno-
ting father and paternal uncle are in odd Bhavas, their well-
being is assured. If the planets denoting mother and maternal
aunt are in even Bhavas, their well being is to be predicted.

29-31. PROCESS OF GROWTH OF EMBRYO AND
LORDS THERE OF : The embryo in the womb improves as
under : First month coagulated blood, second month-mass of
flesh, third month-limbs, fourth month-bones, fifth month-skin,
sixth month-hair, seventh month-movements, eighth month-

feeling of hunger and thirst, ninth month-excitement and
tenth month-riped like a fruit and ready for coming out of the
## Page 98

94 Saravali

womb. These ten months are ruled respectively by Venus,
Mars, Jupiter, the Sun, the Moon, Saturn, Mercury, lord of
Nisheka lagna, the Moon and the Sun. The dispositions of
these lords indicate good or bad of the respective processes.

Notes : Curious readers may refer to Horasara, P. 47
for relevant information.

Balabhadra quotes Parasara as under in this context : The
semen sprinkled in the womb coagulates in the first month. In
the second month it becomesan embryo and assumes the form
of a bubble on water and the sex of the child forms viz. male,
female or eunuch. In the third month it transforms into a
sprout. In the fourth month, the limbs become prominent (well
grown) and the bearing woman develops courage if it is a male
child, assumes timidity if it is a female child and a mixed disposi-
tion if it is a neuter. And the child in the womb also reflects such
dispositions, (Mark the discerning scientific approach of our
sages made thousands of years ago, which may bea news to
even the modern medical scientists !) In the 5th month, blood
strengthens in the child’s body. Bones, hair, nails etc. are added
in the sixth month. During the 7th month, strength and comp-
lexion improves; limbs assume fullness, the child covers the
holes of its ears etc. develops emotions, has a reminiscence of
its previous birth and finds ways and means for Relief. In the
8th month, sound, touch, feeling, etc. occur to the child, and it
develops purity of blood and movements in the womb. Then
in the 9th or the 10th month, delivery takes place.

35-41. ADVERSITIES TO THE PREGNANT WOMAN :
If.at the time of Adhana, the Sun and the Moon are hemmed
between two malefics while the ascendant has no benefic aspect,
the female concerned dies. The same effect prevails if the said
ascendant and the 7th are occupied by malefics and be without
benefic aspect or if the said ascendant is occupied by Saturn
and weak Moon aspected by Mars. Again similar effects shall
come to pass if weak Moon and the Sun are in 12th, Mars in
4th while Venus is between two malefics. Both the child in the
womb and its mother leave this world if malefics occupy the
4th from the said ascendant or from the Moon while Mars is
## Page 100

96 Saravali

in the 7thor Lagoa. The same result follows if Mars is in
4th, Sun in 12th and the Moon be decreasing and be with
malefic aspect. Ifthe Sun is in Lagna while the Moon is weak
or if Mars is in Lagna while malefics are in 12th and 2nd with-
out benefics’ aspect, death occurs of the mother along with
child. The Sun in the 7th at Adhana while Mars is in Lagna,
takes away the child along with its mother through instru-
ments.

Notes : Please see the folowing addition causing death of
the carrying woman : If the 12th house from Adhana Lagna
has malefics, according to Garga, the female dies before deli-
very. Should the Sun and weak Moon be in the 12th, Venus
hemmed between malefics while Mars occupies the 4th, the
female soon quits the world. Malefics in the 4th from Lagna or
the Moon in Adhana chart causes the same effect. Should the
2nd and 12th be aspected by malefics while weak Moon or Mars
or the Sun is in the 12th, the woman passes away prior to her
begetting an issue. The Sun and the Moon connected only
with malefics may also lead to the same conclusion.

42-43, PROGRESS OF PREGNANCY : Should there be
aspects from Mercury, Jupiter, Venus or the Sun to the Lagna,
the process of pregnancy goes on well. The embryo develops
according to the state of the lords of various months (in transit).
In the third month, the pregnant woman develops tastes to eat
various things according to the disposition of the various
monthly lords andLagna Lord and the yogas caused to
them.

Notes : The embryo in te womb develops according to
the planetary transits. If in the 3rd month, the ruler of the
month Jupiter gets adverse influences, its transformation
into a sprout is affected and the embryo may not sustain. Mis-
carriage may follow. If Saturn is afflicted in the 6th month,
## Page 101

Chapter 8 97

deformity of limbs will result. Similar infereaces may be made
as per the transits and months.

The pregnant woman’s taste for eating will vary accord-
ing to various monthly lords. For planetary tastes, see sloka 15,
Ch. 4, infra.

44-45. TIME OF DELIVERY : If at the time of Nisheka
(.e.Adbana) the Sun is in a movable sign, delivery takes place in
the 10th month, if he is in a fixed sign, delivery in 11th month
is indicated and in a dual sign it is in 12th month. If a movable
Rasi ascends at Adhana, delivery takes place in, 10th month,
a fixed Rasi 11th month and dual Rasi 12th month.

Notes: In sloka 45, Rasi may be construed to be Adhana
Lagna or Adhana Chandra Lagna; whichever is stronger
prevails.

The duration of pregnancy is nine solar months or ten
junar months. A solar month is 30 days 26 gh 17 vighatis
32 tatparas and 30 vitatparas. (Sixty units of the latter make
one former.) A lunar revolution takes 27.32 days. The birth
chart can be correlated to coneeption chart, as per the details
given in the Appendix of my English translation of Nashta
Jataka.

The Sun or the Moon or the Lagna—all relating to
Adhana if be ina movable Rasi, delivery takes place in 10th
month; ina fixed Rasi 11th month and ina dual Rasi 12th
month, The Adhana Lagna lord in similar Rasi also leads to
same effect.

Suka Jataka, however, states that delivery will be in 9th
or 10th or llth month according to Adhana Lagna being
movable, fixed or dual siga.

After knowing the possible month, the number of days
will depend on the Horary Moon or Horary Lagna (or Adhana),
Should it be, say, 12° of a sign, delivery will be on the 12th day
of the particular month,
## Page 102

98 Saravali

Also, please see Horasara, page 49 regarding possibile
delivery period.

46-47, The matter of delivery can be guessed through the
Vargas of Nisheka Lagna. The natal Moon can be in the
10th from Adhana Moon. This view is held by many
Acharyas. According to Badarayana, the natal ascendant will
bein the 7th from Adhana Lagna and natal Moon will be in
the 7th from Adhana Moon. Since there are several views

on this, Texplain below (in the next sloka) a view which is
acceptable to all.

Notes : Whatever Rasiis descendent in Nisheka chart
will be the natal ascendant and whichever Rasi is the 7th from
the Adhana Moon will be natal Moon.

Alternatively, the natal ascendant or the natal descendant
will correspond to the Moon at conception. Or the natal
Moon will be over conception ascendant or descendant, If the
Moon be waxing at birth, it will be over conceptional
ascendant and if the natal Moon is waning it will be concep-
tion descendant. The conceptional chart should be worked for
the place where the mother lived at the time of conception.

The number of the days the child spent inthe mother’s
womb can be worked out as under :

(a) It is less than 273 days if the Moon is waxing at birth
and be in the visible half (i. e. between 180 deg-360 deg
from the ascendental cusp.)

(b) It is above 273 days if the Moon is waxing at birth and
be in the invisible half (Lagna to 180 deg).

(c) It is above 273 days if the Moon is decreasing at birth
and bein the visible half.

(d) It is less than 273 days if the Moon is decreasing at
birth and be in the invisible half.

48. VIEW ACCEPTABLE TO ALL ABOUT NATAL
MOON: Note the Dwadasamsa of the Moon at the time of
Adhana. When Moon is so many signs away from her Adhana
position (ina month when delivery is normally possible) deli-
very will take place.

Notes : In horary chart or in conception chart, note
the stronger of the Moon and ascendant. Then find out in
which dvadasamsa it is. If the Moon comes into such dvadasa-
msa in appropriate month, delivery can take place, Let us
assume that the Moon is in Leo in a query chart in 19 deg. It
isin the 8th Dvadasamsa in Pisces. When the Moon transits
pisces in the month concerned, delivery will take place.

Prithuyasas gives some more rules. Please see Horasara
Page 50.

49, BELATED DELIVERY (PREGNANCY): Should a
navamsa of Saturn rule the Nisheka Lagna and Saturn be in
the 7th, the delivery takes place after three years. If Cancer be
the Navamsa Lagna with the Moon in the 7th (from Rasi
lagna) delivery occurs after twelve years.

Notes: As per tne first part of the sloka, Saturn should
occupy the 7th bhava from the ascendant while Capricorn
Navamsa or Aquarius Navamsa be in Lagna. Then, the sexual
act does not promote conception for 3 years to eome. Similarly
if Cancer be the Lagna Navamsa while the Moon occupies the
7th from Lagna, the conception is delayed for 12 years.

Some translators interpret this sloka as well as the
identical ones from Brihat Jataka and Samudra Jataka ina
different way, as if the child remains in the womb for 3 years
or 12 years as the case may be.

100 Saravali

50. FRACTION OF DAY OR NIGHT FOR DELIVERY ;
According to Nisheka Lagna being a day sign or night sign,
delivery will be after so much of fraction of night or day having
passed.

Notes :. Tatkalika Lagna in astrological parlance also
means Prasna Lagna. Hence wherever Tatkalika Lagna is
translated in this chapter as Nisheka Lagna can additionally
mean Prasna Lagna. Such rules may also be horarily applied to.

Now coming to the sloka proper, the time of delivery
during night or day can thus be guessed. If day sign rises at
the time of query (or in Nisheka), birth will be in night time.
Ifnight sign isin Lagna at query (or in Nishcka) then
birth should be declared in day time. Suppose the 10th degree
ofa day sign ison the ascendant; it is one third of Lagna. So,
the birth should be after one third of night is over. This clue
can be used in working out alost horoscope or rectification of
birth time through Prasna.

Day signs are : Leo, Virgo, Libra, Scorpio, Aquarius
and Pisces. Night signs are; Aries, Taurus, Gemini, Cancer,
Sagittarius and Capricorn.

The Moon’s transit as arrived at, as per previous sloka,
may lead lo the knowledge of birth time as instructed in our
present verse.

51-52. Thus should be understood the possible time of
birth in day or night and the Lagna at birth. In similar manner,
the difference between sunrise and birth, i.e. natal ascendant,
and day (week day), fortnight, Muhurta month etc. should be

guessed. Such details relating to birth should first be ascer-
tained and then predictions should be issued with reference to
nativity by astrologers.

53-55. YOGAS FOR EYE DEFECTS : Ifat the time of
Adhana (or at birth), the Sun and Moon are in Leo identical
with Lagna, the child born will be blind; there should be
aspect of Mars and Saturn on Leo. A bubble on the eye should
be predicted if Marsand Mercury aspect the said Sun and
Moon in Leo Lagna. I shall farther explain yogas affecting
the eyes. Should the 12th be occupied by waning Moon, left
eye is destroyed and if by the Sun, it is the right eye. If, how-
ever, benefics aspect (the said 12th and the Sun/Moon), then
by (suitable) efforts, the eye can be repaired.

Notes : Normally th: Sun or Moon in the 12th or 2nd
from Lagma, causes eye defects. If Cancer rises and the Sun be
there, one can find floral mark in the native’s eye.

56. YOGAS FOR DUMBNESS : If malefics are in Rasi
Sandhi aud the Moon is in Taurus aspected by Mars, Saturn
and the Sun, the native born will be dumb. If however there
is benefic’s aspect, the person speaks latter on.

> is with teeth.

58. PECULIAR BIRTH ; Should Mercury be in the Sth
or the 9th from the ascendant while all other planets are devoid
of strength, the child has 2 faces, 4 hands and 4 legs.

59. SHORT STATURE : If the last portion of Capricorn
rises with aspect from Saturn and the luminaries (ie. the Sun
and the Moon), the native is short-statured. The same effect

prevails if the Moon is in Cancer identical with ascendant and
aspected by Mars and Saturn.

60. LAME BY BIRTH : If Pisces rises at birth with aspect

from Mars, Saturn and the Moon, the child born is lame. If

there is a benefic's aspect to the said combination, then relief
can be expected after making efforts.

61. BIRTH WITHOUT HEAD, LEGS AND HANDS :
Should Mars be in the ascendant and fallin the ascendental
decanate or a trinal decanate receiving the aspect of malefics
while benefics are devoid of strength, the child in the womb
develops no head, no legs and no hands respectively.

Notes : If Mars is in the first decanate of Lagna in aspect
to malefics while benefics have no strength, the child will not
have its head, (it may have peculiar head). Similary, the second
decaaate position of Mars in Ligna (i.e. Mars falling in the
5th.from Drekkana Lagaa) with other conditions as laid down
above, the child does not have legs. Again if Mars falls in the
9th from Drekkana Lagna with other rcquirements being ful-
filled as above, the child does not have hands.

1. To know the time of delivery, I have explained the
Adhana chapter. Now I explain the natal chapter as below.

2. KIND OF DELIVERY : If natal Lagna is in Sirshodaya
Rasi, birth is with head foremost, anda Prishtodaya Rasi at
birth indicates birth with legs foremost. The birth is with hands
in such a position ifan Ubhayodaya Rasi ascends. Should
Lagna enjoy benefic aspect, delivery would have been comfor-
table; otherwise difficult.

Notes : Sirshodaya signs are: the signs that ascend with
head first. These are : Gemini, Leo, Virgo, Libra, Scorpio and

- Aquarius, Prishtodaya signs are : Aries, Taurus, Cancer, Sagi-
ttarius and Capricorn. The sign Pisces is called Ubhayodaya
Rasi.

Ifa Seershodaya Rasi (like Leo) rises, the child has come
out of the womb with its head first. Should a Prishtodaya
Rasi (like Cancer) be ascending, the child comes out with legs
first. It comes out with hands first if Pisces be the Lagna.
## Page 108

104 Saravali

If the Moon be with malefics or connected with them,
the delivery would cause difficulty to the mother. Benefics
associated with Lagna makes it easy while malefics indicate
difficulty experienced by mother. According to Maniththacharya,
if the lords of Lagna and Lagna Navamsa are retrograde at
birth, the child birth is with great labour trouble. See (Hora
Ratna Ch. 1).

3-4, PLACE OF DELIVERY : The place of delivery
will correspond to the Rasi Lagna or Navamsa Lagna at birth.
If it is a dual Rasi or Navamsa, delivery will be on the way. A
fixed Rasi/Amsa indicates delivery in one’s own place. Should
the Navamsa be of the same Rasi the delivery is in one’s
own house; otherwise it is otherwise. The delivery will be in
the house of father or mother according to the indicator concer
ned being strong.

be predicted if Lagna and 4th are occupied by benefics, and

8-11 If Scorpio or Cancer ascends with Saturn and is
aspected by Moon, birth is ina deep place. This view is held
by Yavanas and Maniththa. Should Saturn be in watery Rasi
rising and aspected by Mercury, birth isin playground. If the
planet aspecting is the Sun, it is temple and the Moon aspeci-
ting indicates barren lands. Should an “Aranya Rasi” (for
example Leo) be on the Lagna, the birth is in hills, forest,
fortress etc. Should a human Rasi be ascending, and is
aspected by Mars, it is burial ground, if by Mercury sculp-
ture home and if by the Sun cow-shed, royal palace or
temple. If the aspect is from Venus and Mercury, it indicates

pleasing location and if from Venus and Jupiter it is brahmins’
place or where sacred rites are performed.

12. DELIVERY HOME DESCRIBED : Should Jupiter be
exalted in 10th (i.e. Lagna being Libra), delivery is ina 2, 3, or
4 storeyed building. If benefic planets are in Saturn’s Rasi_ or

Navamsa, coinciding with the 4th or 10th, the delivery is in a
veranda or balcony.

13. To know the direction of the delivery room, proceed
thus : One of the dual signs ascending denotes the quarter (of

the direction) in which the room is situated. The other signs
from Aries on indicate the directions of the room,
## Page 110

106 Saravali

Notes : The first two signs preceding the first dual sign
indicate the east. The first dual sign, Gemini, denotes south-
cast. The next dual signs is Virgo denoting south-west. The
signs Cancer and Leo denote the south. The third dual sign
represents north-west while the signs Libra-Scorpio hint at west.
The last dual signs Pisces repersents north-east while Capricorn
and Aquarius indicate the north. Each sign ascending accor-
dingly indicate the direction or quarter in which the delivery
room is located. For example, Virgo rising denotes south-
western room. Similarly other signs.

Notes : Suppose there is astrong planet in the angle of

will denote the direction of delivery room. If Sagittarius with
strength ascends, the building has 3 storeys while strong Capri-
corn indicates a spacious house. The last rules relating to Sagi-
ttarius and Capricorn may always not be found true in a uni-

15, HOUSE OF DELIVERY : If Venus is strong at birth,
itis anew and painted house. Jupiter in strength denotes a
strong house while Mars indicates a burnt house. The Sun
stands for house constructed of wood. It is a new house if the
Moon is strong. Saturn in strength indicates an old house.

18-20. POSITION OF COT : Now explained is the
situation of the cot on which the delivery took place. The 3rd,
6th, 9th and 12th indicate the four legs of cot. ‘The first two
relate to southern side legs and the other two denote the nor-
thera side legs. If the ascendant is aspected by a benefic, the
kind of cloth relating to that benefic was spread on the delivery
cot, The ascendant leads to know the direction in which the
mother was having her head. The depression in the cot corres-
ponds to the common sign occupied by malefics.

21-23. DELIVERY ON GROUND AND NUMBER OF
ATTENDANTS : If the Moon is in her debilitation sign,
identical with the 4th or ascendant, the birth is on the ground
(ec. not on cot, bed etc.) The number of attendants can be
known by the number of planets posited between the Moon
and Lagna. The number of attendants inside the chamber is
known by the number of planets posited in the invisible half and
the number of attendants outside the chamber will correspond
to the number of planets in the visible half. If the concerned
planets are benefic, the attendant ladies are with attractive
features, beautiful and bedecked with ornaments. Malefics
similarly indicate that such females are ugly, unfortunte and
dirty. If the planets are of mixed disposition, but.with strength,
the attending women are in between the said two accounts. Ail
these should be accordingly understood.

24-25. POSITION OF LIGHT : Outof the 12 Rasis the
one occupied by the Sun will indicate the portion of the delivery
chamber where light is kept, If it isfixed sign, the light burns
steadily, and if it is a moving sign, it is unsteady. The portion
that expired in Lagna is indicative of the extent to which the
wick has burnt already. The quantity of oilin the lamp will
correspond to the waxing or waning state of the Moon.

26-21, There were many lights (in the delivery chamber)
if the Sun is aspected by Mars. Should other planets be all

weak, light was obtained by burning grass. Should the Moon

very was in a place of darkness. There is no doubt about this.

Notes ; Since both the Sun and Mars indicate brightness,

and hence the Moon’s connection therewith, lead to birth
without lights. Watery signs are brought in the picture,
Because water is not congenial for a lamp to burn. The con-
juction of the Moon and Saturn in 4th (house related to
mother) also causes darkness at the time of birth.

28-30, BIRTH OUT OF FATHER'S SIGHT : Should the
ascendant be without the aspect of the Moon, the birth is be-
hind the father, i.e. the father was absent from the place. If
the Sun is in the 9th identical with a movable Rasi, the father
was in a foreign place. The Sun in the case of day birth and
Saturn in the case of hight birth, if aspected by Mars, delivery
is out of father’s sight. Ifthe said Sun or Satum be ina
movable sign, death of father (ina distant place) should be
declared. If the Sth, 6th and 7th from the Sun are aspected
or occupied by malefics, the father was under confinement.
Movable, fixed and common signs here indicate confinement,
respectively in foreign place, own place and on the way.

32-33, BIRTHS OUT OF FATHER'S LOINS : The
following lead to birth outside wedlock :

(a) Moon or Lagna sans Jupiter’s aspect.

(b) The luminaries being together without Jupiter’s aspect.

(©) The luminaries along with malefics not receiving the
aspect of Jupiter.

(@) The Sun, the Moon and Jupiter simultaneously in fall
while Saturn is in Lagna and Lagna, Moon and Venus
not being in aspect to Jupiter.

Notes : The following are additional traditional rules for
illegal births =

(1) The Moon in the 4th and in aspect to malefic or ini-
mical planets. (2) Lords of the 3rd, 6th, 2nd and Sth occupying
the ascendant. (3) Saturn in the 10th, malefics in Lagna while
benefics are confined to,the 7th. (4) Mars and Venus in the 3rd
while the Moon is in Lagna (5) Sun in the ascendant and Rahu
in the 4th. (6) Sun and Moon in Lagna or Sun and Mars in
‘7th. (7) Lagna with Mars and Rahu while the luminaries are in
the 7th. (8) No planets in angles, (9) All planets relegated to
2nd, 6th; 8th and 12th (10) Lords of Lagna and 7th in conjun-
tion. (11) Lords of Lagna and 4th in exchange (which is other-
wise a Raga yoga). (12) Lagna and Moon not belonging to
any Varga of Jupiter. (13) The Sun, Moon and Jupiter together
in Lagna while one of them is in fall. (14) Karakamsa Lagna,
related to only malefics. (15) Any one group of the following
prevalent at birth : (a) Sunday-Dvitiya Thithi-Swati Nakshatra
(b) Wednesday-Saptami-Revati, (c) Sunday-Dvadasi-Dhanishta,

Some Of these combinations do not call for literal applica
tion. In this context Jupiter in the 4th or Mars aspecting Jupiter
## Page 115

Chapter 9 il

or any Kendra occupied by a planet or Lagna Lord in Lagna or
benefics aspecting the ascendant or Jupiter and Moon in mutual
Vargas or the Sun and the Moon in exchange cancel the combi-
nations for illegal birth.

34-36. EVILS TO MOTHER: If the Moon is in the 4th or
7th along with malefics, it is evil to mother. The native’s
mother dies (immediately after delivery) if there are malefics in
the 7th from the Moon, and aspected by Mars, The Sun in the
10th from the Moon along with malefics indicate death of the
mother. The same effect prevails if the Sun is in the Sth or 9th
from Venus (??) and with Saturn’s company or aspect. If
birth takes place during night time while Saturn occupies 5th
or 9th from the Moon, the mother soon leaves the world. For
a day birth, if Mars is the Sth or 9th from Venus and aspected
by malefics, the mother dies (early).

Notes : According to Jataka Sarvasva, should the Sun be
in the Sth or the 9th from the Moon and be aspected {by male-
fies, the mother dies carly. If Mars is inthe Sth or 9th from
Venus and aspected by malefics, the paternal grand-mother
dies early.

37-40. MOTHER FORSAKING THE CHILD : If Mars
and Saturn join in the Sth or the 9th from Ascandant, while
the Moon is in the 7th, the child is forsaken by the mother.
Jupiter’s aspect in that case bestows happiness and long
life. The child given up dies if the Moon is in Lagna and Mars
isin the 7th,in aspect to malefics. Mars and Saturnin 11th
bring similar effects. Should a benefic aspect such combinations,
the child is rescued by the respective relative. Both malefics
and benefics aspecting indicate death in the hands of others.
Saturn and Mars joining in the same Amsa indicate that the
child will be forsaken by the mother. Mars in the 7th from the
ascendant in aspect to Saturn produces similar effects.

43-44, COILING BY NAVEL CORD : If the Lagna falls
in a decanate of Mars of Saturn, while malefics or Moon occupy
Lagna, with benefics relegated to 2nd or 11th denote that the
child was born with navel cord coiled around. Should the Sun
be in a quadruped siga, while others with strength remain
in dual (common) signs, it indicates that twins were born
coiled by same navel cord.

1. NEED TO KNOW OF LONGEVITY : In the absence
of knowledge of longevity, attempts to know other information
are futile. So, 1 explain below Arishtas (or evils), in order to
determine longevity.

2. STRENGTH OF MALE AND FEMALE PLANETS :
Male planets are strong in odd Rasis, bright lunar half and
day time. Female planets are strong in even Rasis, dark lunar
half and night time.

plained by astrological expounders. These are: preordained,
accidental and Yogaja (arising of planetary combinations).
The third kind is dealt with below while others are explained
later on,

4, LONGEVITY CURTAILED TO MINIMUM : Should
Jupiter be in the 8th andin a house of Mars (i.e. Aries/Virgo
rising at birth), and aspected by the Sun, the Moon, Mars and
Saturn, the child dies in 3 years.

Notes : For Aries, Jupiter rules the 9th and 12th while
for Virgo, he rules the 4th and 7th houses. Even though he is
aspected by Mars-the dispositior, Saturn-Ayushkaraka and the
luminaries, his close friends, he is harmful in respect of longe-
vity if in the 8th for the said ascendants. If Jupiter is in the 8th
house belonging to Mars, but be without aspect to all the said 4
planets, the longevtiy may be more than 3 years, but not full.

10-11. If Mercury occupies Cancer identical with 6th or 8th
from ascendant and is aspected by the Moon, life is only upto
4, The efficacious Raja Yogas expounded by Yavanas may
produce persons of high descent; even such children are subject
to premature end, in this case.

Notes : For the first rule, the ascendant should either
be Aquarius or Sagittarius, so that Mercury is in 6th or 8th
in Cancer. Thus, the Moon becomes the lord of the 6th for
Aquarius and the lord of the 8th for Sagittarius. Her aspect on
Mereury is deemed to curtail longevity to four years.

In sloka 11, the author hints at the fact that even though
a person may be born with powerful Rajayogas, if Arishta yogas
indicating premature death are simultaneously present, the
latter prevails. Of what use are Rajayogas in the face of
Arishtas ?

31-32. If malefics are in the oriental half of the zodiac,
with benefics relegated to the occidental half, birth in Scorpio
Ascendant causes what is called Vajra Mushti yoga. One bora
in sucha yoga does hardly live. According to Yavanas, if

_ weak Moon is in Lagna while malefics are angular or in the 8th
house (instant) death is caused.*

## Page 125

Chapter 10 121

Notes : The oriental half or eastern half (ie. q¢arm)
in Hindu astrology is the area from the 10th bhava madhya to
the 4th bhava madhya ie. second half of 10th, then the 11th
bhava, 12th, Lagna. 2nd, 3rd and first half of 4th bhava. The
rest of the horoscope i.e. first half of 10th, then the 9th, 8th,
7th, 6th, Sth and the second half of the 4th is called occidental
half or 1% WI of the horoscope. (These two are different from
visible and invisible halves of the chart). In the sloka, the
ascendant is fixed as Scorpio. Hence malefics posited in the
zone of Leo 2nd half through Aquarius first half and benefics
posited in second half of Aquarius through first half of Leo
can cause death at the very boyhood.

33-34, One born in twilight does not live long, if the
ascendant falls in lunar hora, while malefics are posited in the
ead of the Rasis which are angular, along with the Moon.
Should the Moon be amidst two malefis and be in the 7th, 4th
or 8th, even Gods cannot save one from (instant) death.

Notes : Sandhya means the junction of day and night or
the night and day. If one is born at this time while the Lagna
falls in the Hora of Moon (i.e, Lagna being 2nd half of an odd
Rasi or the first half of an even Rasi), and while malefics with
Moon are in the last portions of the Rasis occupied by them,
and be angular, death is early. Individually, the Moon
should not be in the 4th, 7th or 8th hemmed between two
malefics for a long life.

41-42. The Moon, the Sun, Saturn and Mars are capable
of inflicting infant death if they are together in the ascendant,
the 12th, 9th or 8th unaspected by Jupiter of the ascendant is
tenanted by the Sun or the Moon while malefics are in trines
or the 8th and be not aspected by. or conjoined with benefics,
according to Yavanas, infant death is caused.

Notes : As per the first rule, the four planets, viz, the
Sun, the Moon, Mars and Saturn should join either in the
ascendant or in the 8th, or inthe 12th or in the 9th to cause
child mortality. If they are, however, aspected by Jupiter, the
yoga stands nulified, Secondly, when the ascendant is occupied
by the Sun or the Moon while malefics are in th Sth/ 9th/ 8th
without relief from benefics, infant death is indicated.

43-44. Venus joining the Sun and Saturn causes instant
death. This combination doubtlessly gives death in the 9th year
if aspected by Jupiter. Death in childhood occurs if the Moon
is conjoined with Mars, the Sun and Saturn, provided unas-
pacted by benefic planets.

Notes: Should Venus join the Sun and Saturn, the child
will die immediately at birth. If the combination is aspected
by Jupiter, then the longevity is extended upto nine. Similarly
the Moon, Mars, the Sun and Saturn in conjunction will
cause child mortality, if benefics give help, this yoga does.not
prevailand the child will live long, if favourable yogas are
present.

45-46. If the Sun is aspected by Mars and Saturn in the
case of a day birth, it soon leads to death of the father. The
Sun joining malefics (for day birth) also indicates the same
effect. The child’s father and paternal grand father will face
early death if the Sun is in the ascendant along with Mars and
Saturn but unrelated to Mercury, Jupiter and Venus.

Notes: For a native born in day time, the Sun in aspect
to Mars and Saturn or the Sun in the company of malefies (i.e.
Rahu, Ketu, Saturn or Mars) can cause father’s early death.
This is more sure to follow if the house involved is the 9th or
the 10th, If the Sun be in the ascendant with Mars and Saturn,
not connected with Mercury, Venus or Jupiter (or even the
Full Moon aspecting from the 7th), it may kill the father or
gtand-father, Incidentally, if the (Full) Moon in 7th is aspected
by Mars, the Sun and Saturn, unhelped by benefics, it may
prove-adverse for the mother of the child.

47-A8. If the Sun is hemmed between two malefics or is
conjoined with malefics, one born during day time loses his
father early without any doubt. The child’s father at once quits
the world if the planet Sun has Mars and Saturn in the 8th
from him unaspected by benefics.

Notes : The Sun is the indicator of father for day births.
His being free from malefic connections is essential for a long
life of father when the birth takes place during day time.
Similarly, Saturn rules father for night birth and hence he
## Page 129

Chapter 10 125

should be well placed to help the longevity of father in the case
of night birth.

According to the above slokas, if the 8th from the Sun is
occupied by both Saturn and Mars, longevity of the father is
affected. This applies to a day birth.

Inthe case of a night birth, if the Sth from Saturn is
occupied by Mars and Rabu (or even by the Sun), the child’s
father faces quick death. Hence, the 8th house from the Sun
for a day-birth and 8th from Saturn for a night-birth should
be well-disposed so that the father has a long life.

53-54, In the case of night birth, if Saturn is in a movable
sign along with Mars, the father undoubtedly dies in a distant
place. If the Sun joins Mars and Saturn in any Rasi, the father
dies before the birth of the native.

55-56. If malefics are disposed in the Ascendant, 8th,

‘7th, 6th and 12th, the child dies along with its mother. There

is no doubt in it. Should only the 6th and 8th be occupied

by malefics, the mother does not die but the child dies. The

ree is true if malefics are in the ascendant, 8th and the
th.

Notes: Both the child and mother die catly if malefics
are in Lagna, 8th, 7th, 6thand 12th. Only the mother dies
ifthe Lagna, 7th and 8th are occupied by malefics. It is
the child that dics if the 6th and 8th are occupied by malefics.

57-61. YOGAS ADVERSE FOR EYES : Mars or
Saturn in 12th can deprive the native of his eyes—Saturn
right eye and Mars left eye. The native becomes blind
if the Sun andthe Moon are in 12th while 6th and 8th are
occupied by malefics. Even if one among the Sun and the
Moon isin the 12th, damage to eye is indicated; the Sun
affects the right eye while the Moon affects the left one. If
Rahu is in the ascedant while the Sun is in the 7th, the native
is blind by birth. Should the 2nd and the 12th be occupied by
the Moon and the Sun, while malefics are in the 8th and 6th,
person born is blind. If the Moon is in the 6th, the Sun in the
8th, Saturn in the 9th and Mars in the 2nd, simultaneously,
the native is blind. Should the Moon be in the company of
Mars and Saturn and be posited in the 8th or the 6th, the
native loses his eye sight due to bilious and phlegmatic imba-
lances. The said Moon should be conjunct other malefics,
apart from Mars and Saturn. In this combination if the house
involving the Moon is the 8th, the damage is to the right eye
and if it be the 6th, the left eye is damaged. Should, however,
this combination be aspected by bene fics, the damage is not at
birth but will be later on. If the Moon is in the 8th or the 12th
along with Saturn and be aspected by malefics, eye sight is
lost due to windy and phlegmatic complaints—here also, the 8th
## Page 132

128 Saravali

indicates right eye while the 12th the left eye And if benefics
aspect the said Moon in the 8th/12th, the loss is not at birth
but in the course of time, If the Moon is thus associated
with Saturn and the Sun (in several ways), damage to eyes is to
be predicted.

Notes: There are umpteen combinations to know about
eye affictions, thus :

If the 2nd lord joins Venus or is aspected by him or is
trinal or angular to him, adversity of sight should be expected.
‘The same result occurs if the 2nd lord is connected with Lagna
Lord as above. The luminaries in the 2nd cause night-blindness.
Should the lords of Lagna and 2nd house be in an angle along
with the Sun, the child born is blind. Should these join the
the 9th lord, the father becomes blind. (vide Parasara Samhita)

See what Sarvartha Chintamani says in this regard :
Should the lord of the 2nd along with the Lagna lord be in
an evil house, loss of sight is caused. Night-blindness
occurs if Venus and Moon join the 2nd lord. Mars in the
12th damages the left eye. Saturn so posited damages the right
eye. The Sun and Moon in Leo Lagna in aspect to Mars or
Saturn afflict the eyes. Eye diseases are caused ifthe 2nd
lord is conjunct Gulika, Mars and Saturn. If the Navamsa
dispositor of the 2nd lord joins malefics in a malefic Rasi, same
effect prevails.

these houses, cause on the other hand good in respect of ears.

71-73. Whichever Rasi is indicative of a disease shall be
treated as the limb to be afflicted by such disease. The Moon
sign can also be similarly considered. Benefics cause birth
marks on the right or left side of the body according to their
occupation. Should malefics aspect these benefics loss of con-
cerned limb should be expected. Malefics and benefics accord-
ing to their association with the Moon and the visible and
invisible halves (counted from Lagna) cause bad and good
results in this respect.

isin the 3rd asterism from that occupied by the Moon, the

71-82. EFFECTS OF TIME OF STARTING OF DIS-
EASES: The following combinations prevailing at the time

of commencement of a disease cause death in so many days as
indicated :

(1) Malefics in 4th and 8th from Lagna—10 days,

(2) Malefics in 2nd and.12th from Lagna—10 days

(3) The Sun in Sth while Moon is in 9th from -the ascen-
dant—12 days.

(4) The Moon invangle while the Sun is in-4thvor 8th—
3 nights.

(5) The Moon in the 4th while the Sun is in the 6th—
18 days.

(6) The Sun in the Sth or 9th from the Moon—=20 days.

(7) The Sun in the ascendant or the 8th and in aspect to
Saturn and Mars——will finally inflict death.on the
patient.

Notes : If the time of commencement of a disease isnot

properly noted, then the application of these principles and.such
## Page 135

Chapter 10 131
others will lead to pit falls only. For detailed information, see
Ch. 13 of Prasna Marga.

83-88. Mars in Lagna or other angles while Jupiter is
not so, causes death. The Sun in Lagna, Jupiter non-angular
and malefics in the 8th cause immediate death. Similar results
should be predicted if the Moon is in the ascendant, while
Jupiter is ina place other than angles and malefics are in the
8th. Malefics in the 7th from the rising decanate while the Moon
is in the ascendant will also cause death at birth. (In this case,
the Moon shall be in the rising decanate while malefics shall
occupy the 19th decanate). A majority of planets in the 8th—
primarily malefics—indicate longeveity ranging from seven
days to one month. A dead child is born if Saturn is in the
ascendant while Mars is in the 8th, with Jupiter being not in an
angle,

Notes : Mars in Lagna, 4th, 7th or 10th can affect
longevity, if not capable of causing infant death, when Jupiter
does not protect the native by being angular, according to
sloka 83 above. Other principles in the above group of slokas
may accordingly be understood.

89-90. MALEFICS IN RISING DECANATE AND
TRINES THEREOF : Saturn in the rising decanate while a
malefic is in the Sth and another in the 9th—the latter two
should be exactly on trinal decanates as Saturn is—indicates
disease. Mars in the place of Saturn in the said combnation
denotes (infant) death while the Sun so placed indicates disease,
deformity or death.

Notes : If Saturn is in the first decanate of the rising
sign-another malefic in the first decanate in the Sth Risi and yet
another malefic in the 9th Rasi will cause disease of a
serious nature. If Saturn is in the 2nd or 3rd decanate in the
rising sign, then the other malefics referred to should also be
in corresponding decanates. Similarly, Mars replacing Saturn
will denote carly death while the Sun replacing will cause
deformity, disecase or death.

91, DEATH : If at birth Mars is in the ascendant while

Veausis in an angle, Mars causes death when he resumes the
same point in the next round in his transit.

Notes : Let us assume that Mars is in Aquarius ascen-
dant and Venus is in Leo, an angle. After the birth, when Mars
reaches Aquarius again, it is deterimental to the longevity of
the child. So to say, such a child will not live for more than
the period identical with one full course of the zodiac by Mars.

He normally takes fortyfive days to traverse one sign of the
zodiac,

93-97. EXCEEDINGLY LONG LIFE : The native lives
for 108 years if the 8th house is not occupied, while ascendant
is free from malefic residence and Jupiter is in an angle. A span
of over 108 years is granted if Jupiter and Venusare in an angle,
while there are no malefics in trines and the 8th. Predict 120
years of life if Venus is in the ascendant, Jupiter is in an angle
other than the ascendant and the 8th house is not occupied by
malefics. Similar span of life is given if Jupiter isin Caneer
ascendant along with Venus or the Moon while the 8th house
is not occupied. If angles, trines and the 8th house are not
occupied by malefics, one’s longevity is comparable to that of
Gods.

98. ELAPSED LONGEVITY : Weak Moon along with
malefics if posited in the 8th, 7th, 12th, Ist, Sth or 9th and
unaspected by benefics will only grant elapsed longevity, i.e.
immediate death.

the said houses, without benefic aspect is capable of causing
death in childhood.

99, TIMING INFANT DEATH: When the child with
powerful infant mortal combinations is in its first year, death
will come to pass if the Moon with strength passes over the
natal position of another qualified planet, or on its own natal
position (i.e, Janma Rasi) or natal ascendant. In all these cases,
the Moon should be aspected by malefios.

Notes : The sloka gives clue to the effect of finding out
the day of death in case of powerful child mortality. The Moon
with strength in transit if moves over her own natal position or
over the natal ascendant or over another planet’s natal position
capable Of curtailing longevity can cause the end of the
child.

100-103. DEATH IN CHILDHOOD : Any one group of
the following planets’ joining in one house will cause death in
five years: (1)-The Sun, the Moon, Mars and Jupiter (2) Mars,
Jupiter, Saturn and the Moon (3) The Sun, Saturn, Mars and
the. Moon. Even if a child is on the God’s laps, it will die in
Tith year if the Sun conjunct Mercury is aspected by malefics.
Death within 7 years of age will occur if the Sun is in the
ascendant along with Mars and Saturn while declining Moon
## Page 139

Chapter 10 135)

isin the 7th in a house owned by. Venus, provided this combi-
nation is not aspected by Jupiter: Should the Sun and the
declining-Moon be in angles‘and be conjanct with or in aspect
to Mars and Saturn, the child has a longevity of only 4 years.
In these cases, i.e. where child mortality is indicated, there is no
use of making any calculations.

Notes : Each group of planets as above being together at
birth can cause child mortality. The Sun and Mercury being in
conjunction and in aspect to severe malefics can cause death in
the eleventh year. If the ascendant is Aries or Scorpio, and is
occupied by the Sun, Mars and Saturn waile the 7th house is
tenanted by declining Moon (i.e. the lunisolar angle being less
than 180 degrees), death in the 7th year is denoted. Jupiter’s
aspect (on the 7th or the ascendant) is a redeeming feature. The
‘Sun in one angle; the Moon of dark half in another angle (i.0.
the Moon with diminishing angular distance with reference to
the Sun-for example when the Sun is in the 10th, dark half
Moon can be in the 7th), and the company of or aspect to
Mars and Saturn (i.e. Mars and Saturn can individually be:
connected with the luminaries or both of them either connected
with the Sun or the Moon), the 4th year of age will be fatal
for the child. The author says that when child. mortality is
powerful in the horoscope, no other calculations need be made
in the matter of longevity.

104. DEATH IN THIRD YEAR: If waning Moon or
Lagna Lord be in the Marana Pada and aspected by all the
malefics, but not benefics, the length of life is only 3 years.

Not Maranapada has been interpreted as 8th house
by some. But it actually means the Rasi counted so many signs
away from the Rasi in which the 8th lord is as he is away
from the'8th. Note how many signs away the 8th lord is from
the 8th, So many Rasis away from the 8th lord’s Rasi is
Marana Pada, For example, take a Capricorm native, His 8th
## Page 140

136 Saravali

Rasi is Leo lorded by the Sun, Assume that the Sun (8th
Lord) is in Aries, ic. 9 Rasis away from Leo, the 8th. So
count 9 Rasis from Aries, the Sun sign. We get Sagittarius,
thus, as Marana Pada.

death before the age of 12 is denoted.

108-110. If Rahu is in Aquarius, Leo or Scorpio identical
with the ascendant and is aspected by malefics, the life span is
only 7. If Dhuma Ketu rises followed by fall of meteor and
strong gale and if birth occurs in Raudra Muhurta or Sarpa
Muhurta, the subject invites early death.

Notes : Rudara Muhurta is for four ghatis Sun-rise while
‘Sarpa Muhurta rules for 48 minutes from Sun set. If declining
Moon is conjunct malefics, aspecting Rahu, death within few

111-114. FATEFUL DEGREES OF THE MOON: The
Moon is capable of inflicting death ifshe is in any of the
following degrees at birth: Aquarius 21°, Leo 5°, Taurus 9°,
Scorpio 23°, Aries 8°, Cancer 12°, Libra 4°, Capricorn 20°,
Virgo 1°, Sagittarius 18, Pisces 10° and Gemini 22°. If the
Moon is in such degrees at birth, death is indicated in the
corresponding year and the native cannot be protected by even
God Yama.

Notes: Should the Moon be in any degree as above,
death occurs in the corresponding year. For example, if the
Moon is in 23 degrees of Scorpio, the person dies at the age
of 23.

Horasara states that the fateful degrees for the Moon
from Aries onwards are 26, 12,13, 25, 24, 4, 26, 14, 13, 25,
Sand 12 and the same for Lagna are from Aries onwards: 8,
29,22, 22, 25,14, 4, 23,18, 20, 21 and 10, Phala Deepika
(Chg 13) has the same view of Prithuyasas.

Jataka Tatwa (B-138) also denotes fateful degrees for the
Moon from Aries onwards respectively thus : 8,9, 23, 22, 5,
1, 4, 23, 18, 20, 21 and 10, These are death inflicting degrees in
the respective year of age.

‘These can be used in horary also relating to questions on
death of an ailing person.

3-4, If the Moon is Full and is aspected by all heavenly
bodies, all evils are countered just as lawbreakers are destroyed
by the king. Venus aspecting the Full Moon while the latter is
in friendly divisions is capable of obstructing evils just as
abdomenal remedies are able to cure windy diseases.
Notes : The full Moon in aspect to all planets is capable
of nullifying evils against longevity If she is full and is aspected
by Venus, then also the evils for short life will vanish, In the
latter: case, the Moon should simultancomsly be in friendly
divisions. wd

6-7. A benefic planet victorious in planetary war at birth
and essentially aspected by another benefic, destroys all evils
just as gale can uproot trees. If a’planet has a halo (in the sky)

and is aspected by a malefic, evils are countered just as the
solar eclipse day bath in Kurukshetra does.

Notes : There must be a benefic involved in planetary
war and must be victorious and be in aspect to another benefic,
Then only, the yoga comes to pass. Two planets are said to
in war (except the Sun and the Moon), when they are in con-
junction and within a longuitude of one degree. The one with
less longidude wins the war. For example, Jupiter and Mercury
are in Taurus at 24° 10’ and 24° 29’ respectively. Jupiter is
declared successful as he is behind Mercury.

is always close to the sage Vasishta. The star Marichi is in
the east, Vasishta is to His West, Atri is to the west of Vasi-

Kratu.

12, If at birth, many planets are capable of giving
benefic results, even then there is no blemish just as the king
gets success in journey undertaken when the Moon is in a trine
to the Sun.

Notes : There are two important clues in this sloka.
Firstly, if a majority of planets are beneficial to the native, the
other malefic combinations get nullified. Here is a clue to the
effect that awisdom-based judgement is necessary-in astrology
and rushing to conclusion by surface study is detrimental. The
second clue is: if the Moon is trine the Sun, at the time of a
query, success in journey is indicated.

14. If Jupiter and the Moon be in Cancer, identical
with 4th, 10th, or the ascendant, Mercury and Saturn be in
Libra while others are in the 11th, 3rd and 6th, one has
illimitable longevity.

Notes: The Moon and Jupiter. should be in Cancer as

Cancer for Libra ascendant. Additionally, Saturn should be
exalted joining Mercury, while the Sun, Venus and Mars should
confine to the 3rd, 6th or 11th from Lagna. This rare yoga
bestows a very long lease of life on the native concerned.

15. Ihave thus explained the Yogas that are capable
of countering the evils, as laid down by our great ancestors.
May the astrologers please the king with the knowledge of
these.

Notes : The yogas explained in this and the previous
chapter are guidelines only to know the combinations that
counter child or infant mortality and relate only to longevity. As
already cautioned, these do not necessarily work for all kinds
of defects as antidotes. For example, a certain combination
explained in this context will not necessarily offset an imbalance
in one’s education, marriage, progeny etc.

Chapter 13 Lunar Yogas

qrarsanr-geaet Haha ae: wa Te kea: |
faarataaded: Sraarareranteat: ug

1. SUNAPHA, ANAPHA AND DURUDHURA YOGAS :
Excepting the Sun, aay other planet in the 2nd from the Moon
causes Sunapha yoga, in the 12th Anapha yoga and in both the
2nd and the 12th Durudhura yoga.

Notes : Just as the Sun, the nodes are also not considered
in this kind of Raja yogas.

The Moon should have a planet either in the 12th or in
the 2nd (or at least with it) so that she remains balanced.
Otherwise, Kemadruma yoga is caused, as could be seen in
the following verses and notes thereof. Unless the Moon is
thus well-balanced, the native is not likely to feel comfortable
in life. He will face only obstacles in day-to-day affairs. The
said 3 yogas as per the present sloka are caused only by Mars,
Mercury, Jupiter, Venus and Saturn. ach position by a
different planet manifests varied effects, vide infra.

Ua waar aie: Feragatora: TANGA 1
Sageistrnce: ata  aaeaagtest ue

2. KEMADRUMA YOGA : Kemadruma yoga is formed
if at least one of the said three yogas (viz. Sunapha, Anapha
and Durudhura yogas) is not present or if the Moon’s angles
are devoid of planets or if she is unaspected by all the planets.
Such yoga causes extreme difficulties,

Notes : Elaborate notes and comments can be found in
my English translation of Horasara (P, 230) which the reader
may consult,
## Page 153

Chapter 13 149

Kalyana Varma uses amea agies? thereby requiring the
Moon to be in aspect to all planets in deviation to standard
textual versions. As otherwise, he states, the Moon produces
Kemadruma yoga This condition is quite strange.

grarrarsenticrtata (30) feaagut afte:(gco) 1
ae ategerai searefaet = aareqrar: zu

3, DIFFERENT PERMUTATIONS : By all possible
permutations and transmutations, one can see 30 kinds of
Sunapha yoga, 30 kinds of Anapha yoga and 180 kinds of
Durudhura yoga.

Notes : We have learnt that any planet other than the
Sun in the 2nd of the Moon causes Sunapha yoga, Foa example
Mars in the 2nd of the Moon causes Sunapha yoga. Similarly,
the other four i.e. Mercury, Jupiter, Venus and Saturn indi-
vidually cause Sunapha yoga. Thus 5S kinds of this yoga is
formed in the first instance, With group of two, these 5
planets can severally form 10 kinds of additional Sunapha
yoga. For example Mars plus Mercury or Mars plus Jupiter or
Mars plus Venus and so on and forth. This is the second set
of 10 permutations. In group of 3 each, these 5 planets can
form again ten permutations in the third instance. For exmple,
Mars + Mercury +Jupiter or Mars-+Mercury+Venus and so
on and so forth. In the 4th instance, these 5 planets in group
of4 each can cause 5 different permutations, such as Mars+
Mercury +-Jupiter-+Venus or Mars + Mercury +Jupiter + Saturn
etc. Inthe Sth instance all the 5 planets in the 2nd give rise
to one transmutation. Thus these 5 different transmutations
cause in their order 5+-10+10+5+1=31 kinds of Sunapha
yoga.

Same transmutations can be conceived with these 5 planets
in the 12th for Anapha yoga also and we get 31 different yogas.
Similarly, disposing these 5 planets in the 2nd and 12th in
group of | to 5, we can conceive 180 kinds of Durudhura yoga
transmutations.

Parasara in his Brihat Parasara Hora Sastra (ch. 37; sloka
13-my English translation) observes thus: The yogas (like
## Page 154

150 Saravali

Sunapha, Anapha, Durudhura, Kemadruma, Chandradhi yoga
etc.) prevail over the other good or bad yogas in the horoscope.
Hence one must beforehand analyse the good and -bad effects
of yogas from the Moon.

ata crargiawal agadaita:
arearifagagaar: = eagurfrea:

gat: gary fagaet: gaerfrara neu

4. EFFECTS OF SUNAPHA YOGA: One born with
Sunapha yoga will be wealthy, will have self-made prowess
(or will reach an exalted position of his own efforts), be very
virtuous, be learned in Sastras and their meanings, be very
famous, virtuous (like Lord Rama)!, be peacefully disposed,
happy, be a king or a minister and be highly intelligent.

Notes: The word q@t apart from meaning “happy”
has various meanings like : agreeable, charming, sweet, joyful
etc.

One born with Sunapha yoga will be a king or equal to
a king, be wise, rich, famious and will earn wealth by his own
efforts, (vide my English translation of Brihat Parasara Hora
Sastra ch. 37, sloka 8). Prithuyasas in Horasara (Ch. 19) also
adds that this yoga gives self-made wealth. The native will
have rich knowledge of Sastras and be a commentator thereof.

Jatakabharana in chapter on “Chandrayogas” asserts
that the native will have self-made wealth, will enjoy fame,
wisdom, and all kinds of happiness, be a scholar and a minister
of the king.

Thus, planets other than the Sun in the 2nd house counted
from the Moon promote the prospects of the native’s having
self made riches. If the planet in question be Venus or Jupiter
or Mercury, the subject can earn a fair amount of wealth,
Exalted Saturn or exalted Mars will also give good results in
this regard.

5. EFFECTS OF _ANAPHA YOGA : One. born. in
Anapha yoga will be eloquent in speech, magnanimous,, virtu-
ous, will enjoy food, drink, flowers, robes and females, . will be
famous, calm (aatfga) in disposition, happy, pleased. and will
possess a beautiful body.

Notes: According to Brihat Parasara Hora Sastra (ch:
37), this yoga makes one a king, free from diseases, blessed
with all kinds of happiness, virtuous, famous and beautiful.

One born in Anapha yoga will have political wisdom and
moral training, be steadfast, will know many sastras) be blessed
with cnormous wealth, be capable of attracting the fair sex
and be honoured (vide P. 228 of of Horasara.) Thus, this yoga
gives plenty of wealth, if for example 12th from Moon is
occupied, particularly by exalted Venus; or when the Moon is
in Leo while Jupiter is in Cancer; or when Mercury is in Virgo.
with Moon in Libra.

Dundhiraja in his Jatakabharana also praises Anapha
yoga. The effects are : good conduct, kingly status, beauty
etc.

The Anapha and Sunapha caused by a debilitated planet
will only yield adverse results, Forexample when the Moon
is in Libra with Venus in 12th in Virgo, Anapha yoga produces
only immoral “conduct instead of good conduct. Such natives
cannot enjoy physical comforts, long life etc.

6. EFFECTS OF DURUDHURA YOGA : One born
in Durudhura yoga will be famous on the earth for his speech,
wisdom, valour and virtues. He will enjoy freedom, comforts,
wealth and conveyances. He will be liberal but will come to
grief by maintaining his family members. He will have good
behaviour.

Notes : One born with this yoga, will enjoy the comforts
generated by him, be charitable, and be endowed with wealth,
conveyances and attendants (See ch. 37 of BRIHAT
PARASARA HORA SASTRA).

According to Horasara, P. 228, such a native will enjoy
luxuries and wealth. He will be an eloquent speaker, be fond
of battles and be an army chief. He will be in a state of
bewilderness, be kingly and sacrifying in nature. He will
have cattle,

Vide Jatakabharana, the native will enjoy wealth,
conveyances, lands etc., be equal toa king and be happy with
women,

Compared to Sunapha and Anapha yogas, Durudhura
yoga is more effective as it is not that frequent to occur. The
Moon gets enormous strength to yield good effects if she is
Planked by planets on both the sides. The native, according
to Parasara, is destined to experience comforts of his own.

7. EFFECTS OF KEMADRUMA YOGA : The
native with Kemadruma yoga will be deprived of wife, drinks,
food, residence, robes and friends, though he may belong to
regal scion, He will suffer from poverty, grief, sickness and be
dirty. He will live by hard labour, be wicked and be inimi-
cally disposed to one and all.
## Page 157

Chapter 13 153

Notes : The native with this yoga will be blameworthy,
be devoid of intelligence and learning and will experience
penury and misfortunes, vide BRIHAT PARASARA HORA
SASTRA, ch. 37, sloka 12, Prithuyasas in Horasara emphati-
cally declares that even a king with this position will beg
(p. 230).

According to Jatakabharana, one with this yoga will
resort to unacceptable professions, be dirty, will present
himself in bad dress, be a servant, will live in distant countries,
and be devoid of wife, sons, friends and money even though
he may be of a royal scion,

Manasagari, however, attributes long life to the native
while describing other bad effects. It adds that the said
Kemadruma is defunct if the Moon is in a. benefic’s Rasi and
is conjoined with Mercury or Venus or Jupiter.

8-9. OTHER KIND OF SUNAPHA ETC.: The kind
of Sunapha yoga etc arising from the Moon’s angles are (also)
important. ‘These yogas give effects according to the state of
the Moon (ie. depending on her rays, being Full, New etc.).
The strength of the planets, viz. Mars etc. causing these yogas,
native’s country and the race he belongs to must be properly
understood before evaluating Sunapha etc.

Notes : A different set of Sunapha etc. may be noted
as under :

If a planet other than the Sun is in the 4th of the
Moon, Sunapha yoga is formed. Similarly the 10th house
position causes Anapha and occupations of both the 4th and
10th cause Durudhura yoga. This account is given by Srutakirti.

Another view is of Jeevasarman which indicates that the
## Page 158

154 Saravali

2nd and 12th houses in the Navansa chart with reference to
the Moon shall be considered for these yogas.

It seems that Srutakirti’s yogas too have meaning in this
context.

10-11, RESULTS OF SUCH YOGAS CAUSED BY
MARS ETC. : If Sunapha yoga is caused by Mars (by being in
the 2nd of the Moon), the native will be valorous, wealthy,
cruel in speech, be an army chief, will be fierce, torturous,
proud and inimical. If Mercury be the cause of Sunapha
yoga, the native will be expert in Vedas, Sastras and music.
He will be virtuous, and a poet. He will be high-minded,
intent on thinking of good for all and will possess a brillant
physique.

Notes: Sunapha yoga caused by different planets from
Mars to Saturn have different effects. While analysing a given
horoscope, these effects further vary according the Rasi involved
and the lordships of the planet concerned. For example, Mars
may cause Sunapha yoga for a Capricorn native which can
give enormous wealth while for a Virgo native this planet will
only .give very ordinary wealth as he is the lord of the 8th
also,

Jataka Parijatha, ch. 7, slokas 86 and 87 attribute
similar results as per Kalyana Varma for Mars and Mercury
individually causing this yoga. According to Manasagari,
this yoga by Mars causes perennial enmity with others. For
Mercury same results as per our text and Jataka Parijatha
are mentioned.

In fact, Manasagari and Jataka Parijata have exactly
followed our author's views for effects of Sunapha, Anapht
and Durudhura yogas by various planets.

15-19. ANAPHA YOGA'S EFFECTS GIVEN BY MARS
ETC.: If Anapha yoga is caused by Mars-being in the 12th from

splendorous, famous and will have abundant gold. If Saturn
causes this yoga, the subject will be broad-shouldered, be a

quadrupeds, devoted to an infamous lady and be virtuous,

30, LUNAR YOGAS FROM THE SUN: If the Moon
is in an angle [rom the Sun, little effects will be felt in regard to
money, wisdom, skill, learning and modesty. These are medium
if the Moon be in Panaphara (i.e. 2nd, Sth, 8th and 11th) and
exceedingly good in Apoklima (i.e. 3rd, 6th, 9th and 12th).

Notes : Should the Moon be in the 6th or 12th from the
Sua, she promotes one’s learning, wealth, wisdom etc.

Phala Deepika designates these yogas (vide ch. 6, sloka 14)
thus : The Moon in an angle of the Sun causes Adhama’ yoga;
## Page 163

Chapter 13 159

in Panaphara it causes Sama (a4) yoga and in Apoklima, the
yoga is termed as Varishta yoga. The results ascribed are
(sloka 18)—wealth, conveyances, fame, happiness, intelligence,
wisdom, learning etc. in little quantity for Adhama yoga, in
medium quantity for Sama yoga (aqatt) and the highest for
Varishta yoga.

31. MOON IN VISIBLE AND INVISIBLE HALVES :
Tn the case of a night birth, if the Moon is with Parivesha
(halo), and be declining in the invisible half of the zodiac
(ie. being posited between Lagna Bhava Madhya and the
centre of the descendant-7th house), or declining Moon in day
time be in the visible half (ie. between the centres of the
descendant and the ascendant), even results will be felt in
respect of fear, grief etc. (That is. these positions confer bad
results). The Full Moon gives kingdom, if she be contrarily
posited.

Notes: The Full Moon in the case of day birth in the
invisible half and ia the case of night birth in the visible half
confers kingdom,
